How I made it (I know this was uploaded years ago but who cares): 1. Take a pen  2. Open the pen and put the ink stick sorta thing somewhere 3. Take water 4. Take glitter or whatever you want.  5. IF YOUR TAKING GEL THeN DO NOT USE water. 6. Put water in pen, put glitter/ whatever in and close it 7. If you have holes at the end of your pen then use glue and leg it harden 8. After it's hard, it's a solid now and can prevent water falling on your pages when your writing    Thanks!

Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµÑ€ĞµÑÑĞ½Ğ¾ ĞµÑ‰Ñ‘ Ñ€ÑƒÑĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ğ·Ğ´ĞµÑÑŒ ĞµÑÑ‚ÑŒ???
GUYS SOME THINGS KARINA SAID TO DO DIDN'T WORK && HAD TO BE IMPROVISED:   Baby Oil && Food Colouring mixed with water didn't work && the water just stayed @ the bottom. I used all the different ratios I could && nothing worked.   -The beads don't exactly float. depends on what kind && they need to be rounded.  If they're not rounded, the they'll pack together which is still cool, but if you want that "orbeez" effect, then they have to be rounded.   The Cork Didn't really become "squishy" as she claimed, && it was extremely hard. Maybe it's the cork or needle I used,  but be careful.   When the model magic clay dries, apply a layer of mod podge over it to protect it from crumbling or "melting" bc if it touches any liquid, it'll leave cracks && creases.   Don't get me wrong I love these DIYs but if any of you attempt it, here are some things that didn't work out (for me) For more info, or questions, DM @kats.apparel on Instagram :))

You did something  different  from hellomaphei
warning in advance for anybody who wants to do this - i've heard lots of folks who make small charms with those glass bottles say that clear glue and other liquids can either discolor over time or evaporate through the stopper completely. to keep the latter from happening, you can apply a coat or two of nail varnish to the bottom of your cork, creating a seal!  since it's a pen tho it would probably get used up before that happens anyway, haha  additionally, putting glue on the end of the ink cartridge may prevent ink from flowing and ultimately give your pen a rather short life span, since no air can displace the ink that's being used. don't quote me on this tho but when it comes down to it, this is a fun craft with a pretty outcome and that's what matters! have fun using your pens, friends! <3
